{"nick":"joepie91","message":"SGrover: as for the scalability trap thing... there's no such thing as arbitrary scalability - any kind of (horizontal) scalability involves a tradeoff somewhere else, usually in reliability... so if you try to design something to be arbitrarily scalable, all you'll end up doing is making a ton of tradeoffs, 95% of which you'll never need to do because that bit doesn't need to be scaled horizontally, and after a few months you'll discover that it","date":"2019-02-27T18:35:41.062Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"isn't as universally scalable as you thought it was, and now you have to restructure all of your code anyway","date":"2019-02-27T18:35:42.516Z","type":"message"}
